return `${estado||'Pendiente'}`; } function roleBadge(role) { const m = { admin:'badge-admin',coordinador:'badge-coord',gestor:'badge-gestor',contratista:'badge-contratista' }; return `${role||'—'}`; } function isMonthReached(mes) { if (!mes) return false; const idx = MESES.indexOf(mes); if (idx < 0) return true; return new Date() >= new Date(2026, idx, 1); } function munList(cap) { if (!cap.municipios || !cap.municipios.length) return '—'; return cap.municipios.map(m => m.nombre||m).join(', '); } function ipsList(cap) { if (!cap.ips || !cap.ips.length) return '—'; return cap.ips.map(i => i.nombre||i).slice(0,2).join(', ') + (cap.ips.length>2?'…':''); Math.round(exec/total*100) : 0; document.getElementById('s-total').textContent = total; document.getElementById('s-exec').textContent = exec; document.getElementById('s-pend').textContent = pend; document.getElementById('s-part').textContent = part; document.getElementById('s-muni').textContent = munis.size; document.getElementById('s-cumpl').textContent = total ? cumpl+'%' : '—'; const upcoming = allCaps .filter(c => c.estado!=='Ejecutado' && c.estado!=='Cancelado') .sort((a,b)=>MESES.indexOf(a.mesProgramado)-MESES.indexOf(b.mesProgramado)) .slice(0,8); const tb = document.getElementById('dash-table'); if (!upcoming.length) { tb.innerHTML='Sin próximas capacitaciones'; return; } tb.innerHTML = upcoming.map(c => ` ${c.tema} ${areaLabel(c.area)} ${c.mesProgramado||'—'} ${munList(c)} ${c.modalidad||'—'} ${badge(c.estado||'Pendiente')} ${isMonthReached(c.mesProgramado)&&canEdit(c.area)? ``: 'No disponible aún'} `).join(''); const readyN = allCaps.filter(c=>isMonthReached(c.mesProgramado)&&c.estado!=='Ejecutado'&&c.estado!=='Cancelado').length; const be = document.getElementById('badge-exec'); be.textContent = readyN; be.style.display = readyN ? 'inline-block' : 'none'; } // ── PLANEACION ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── window.renderPlan = function() { const areaF = document.getElementById('f-area').value; const mesF = document.getElementById('f-mes').value; const estF = document.getElementById('f-estado').value; const natF = document.getElementById('f-nat').value; const searchF = document.getElementById('f-search').value.toLowerCase(); let caps = allCaps.filter(c => { if (areaF && c.area!==areaF) return false; if (mesF && c.mesProgramado!==mesF) return false; if (estF && (c.estado||'Pendiente')!==estF) return false; if (natF && !(c.ips||[]).some(i=>i.naturaleza===natF)) return false; if (searchF && !c.tema.toLowerCase().includes(searchF)) return false; return true; }); const tb = document.getElementById('plan-table'); if (!caps.length) { tb.innerHTML='Sin registros'; return; } tb.innerHTML = caps.map((c,i)=>` ${i+1} ${c.tema}

((parseFloat(c.postest)-parseFloat(c.pretest)).toFixed(1)+'%') : '—'; return ` ${i+1} ${c.tema} ${areaLabel(c.area)} ${munList(c)} ${ipsList(c)} ${c.mesProgramado||'—'} ${c.mesEjecucion||'—'} ${c.participantes||'—'} ${c.pretest!=null?c.pretest+'%':'—'} ${c.postest!=null?c.postest+'%':'—'} ${cambio} ${badge(c.estado||'Pendiente')} `; } const filtered = allCaps.filter(inPeriod); const total = filtered.length; const exec = filtered.filter(c=>c.estado==='Ejecutado').length; const part = filtered.reduce((a,c)=>a+(parseInt(c.participantes)||0),0); Municipios

${pct}% `; }).join(''); // Por municipio const munMap = {}; filtered.forEach(c=>{ (c.municipios||[]).forEach(m=>{ const k = m.nombre||m; if (!munMap[k]) munMap[k]={caps:0,part:0,ips:new Set(),nats:[]}; munMap[k].caps++; munMap[k].part += parseInt(c.participantes)||0; (c.ips||[]).forEach(i=>{ munMap[k].ips.add(i.nombre||i); if(i.naturaleza) munMap[k].nats.push(i.naturaleza); }); }); }); const tb2 = document.getElementById('inf-muni-table'); const sorted = Object.entries(munMap).sort((a,b)=>b[1].caps-a[1].caps); if (!sorted.length) { tb2.innerHTML='Sin datos'; return; } tb2.innerHTML = sorted.map(([mun,d])=>{ const natCount = d.nats.reduce((acc,n)=>{acc[n]=(acc[n]||0)+1;return acc},{}); const dominante = Object.entries(natCount).sort((a,b)=>b[1]-a[1])[0]?.[0]||'—'; return `${mun}${d.caps}${d.part}${d.ips.size}${dominante}`; }).join(''); }; // ── TYPEAHEAD: MUNICIPIOS ────────────────────────────────────────────────────── window.filterMunicipios = function() { const q = document.getElementById('mun-input').value.toLowerCase().trim(); const dd = document.getElementById('mun-dropdown'); if (!q) { dd.innerHTML=''; dd.classList.remove('open'); return; } // Deduplicate municipios by nombre const seen = new Set(); const unique = MUNICIPIOS_DATA.filter(m=>{ if(seen.has(m.nombre)){return false;} seen.add(m.nombre); return true; }); const results = unique.filter(m=>m.nombre.toLowerCase().includes(q)).slice(0,10); if (!results.length) { dd.innerHTML='
